#Create a simulator object
set ns [new Simulator]

#Define different colors for data flows (for NAM)
$ns color 1 Red
$ns color 2 Blue
$ns color 3 Green
$ns color 4 Yellow
$ns color 5 Black

#Open the NAM trace file
set nf [open /home/lucas/Documents/ns2/nsOutput/afterupload46_scriptNS2_0416802013.nam w]
$ns namtrace-all $nf

#Define a 'finish' procedure
proc finish {} {
	global ns nf
	$ns flush-trace
	#Close the NAM trace file
	close $nf
	exit 0
}

#Server Moodle
set internet [$ns node]
set server [$ns node]
$ns duplex-link $internet $server 100Mb 60ms DropTail

#Create nodes Polo 1
set S1 [$ns node]
$ns simplex-link $internet $S1 20Mb 50ms DropTail
$ns simplex-link $S1 $internet 9.200000000000001Mb 50ms DropTail

#Create connection TCP Polo 1


#Polo 1 Maquina 1 -- Servidor
set tcpP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP1M1ToServer set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $tcpP1M1ToServer
set sinkP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP1M1ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP1M1ToServer $sinkP1M1ToServer
$tcpP1M1ToServer set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP1M1ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP1M1ToServer attach-agent $tcpP1M1ToServer
$ftpP1M1ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 1 Maquina 1
set tcpServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M1 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M1
set sinkServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$tcpServerToP1M1 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M1 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M1 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M1
$ftpServerToP1M1 set type_ FTP

$ftpP1M24ToServer attach-agent $tcpP1M24ToServer
$ftpP1M24ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 1 Maquina 24
set tcpServerToP1M24 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M24 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M24
set sinkServerToP1M24 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M24 $sinkServerToP1M24
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M24 $sinkServerToP1M24
$tcpServerToP1M24 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M24 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M24 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M24
$ftpServerToP1M24 set type_ FTP

$ns connect $tcpP3M14ToServer $sinkP3M14ToServer

#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP

$ftpP3M14ToServer attach-agent $tcpP3M14ToServer
$ftpP3M14ToServer set type_ FTP

#Polo 4 Maquina 7 -- Servidor
set tcpP4M7ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP4M7ToServer set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $P4M7 $tcpP4M7ToServer
set sinkP4M7ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP4M7ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP4M7ToServer $sinkP4M7ToServer
$tcpP4M7ToServer set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP4M7ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP4M7ToServer attach-agent $tcpP4M7ToServer
$ftpP4M7ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 4 Maquina 7
set tcpServerToP4M7 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP4M7 set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP4M7
set sinkServerToP4M7 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P4M7 $sinkServerToP4M7
$ns connect $tcpServerToP4M7 $sinkServerToP4M7
$tcpServerToP4M7 set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP4M7 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP4M7 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M7
$ftpServerToP4M7 set type_ FTP

$ftpServerToP4M46 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M46
$ftpServerToP4M46 set type_ FTP

#Polo 4 Maquina 47 -- Servidor
set tcpP4M47ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP4M47ToServer set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $P4M47 $tcpP4M47ToServer
set sinkP4M47ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP4M47ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP4M47ToServer $sinkP4M47ToServer
$tcpP4M47ToServer set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP4M47ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP4M47ToServer attach-agent $tcpP4M47ToServer
$ftpP4M47ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 4 Maquina 47
set tcpServerToP4M47 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP4M47 set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP4M47
set sinkServerToP4M47 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P4M47 $sinkServerToP4M47
$ns connect $tcpServerToP4M47 $sinkServerToP4M47
$tcpServerToP4M47 set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP4M47 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP4M47 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M47
$ftpServerToP4M47 set type_ FTP

$ftpP3M28ToLS3 attach-agent $tcpP3M28ToLS3
$ftpP3M28ToLS3 set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 3 Maquina 28
set tcpLS3ToP3M28 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpLS3ToP3M28 set class_ 3
$ns attach-agent $P3LS $tcpLS3ToP3M28
set sinkLS3ToP3M28 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P3M28 $sinkLS3ToP3M28
$ns connect $tcpLS3ToP3M28 $sinkLS3ToP3M28
$tcpLS3ToP3M28 set fid_ 3
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpLS3ToP3M28 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpLS3ToP3M28 attach-agent $tcpLS3ToP3M28
$ftpLS3ToP3M28 set type_ FTP

set tcpP3M47ToLS3 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP3M47ToLS3 set class_ 3
$ns attach-agent $P3M47 $tcpP3M47ToLS3
set sinkP3M47ToLS3 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P3LS $sinkP3M47ToLS3
$ns connect $tcpP3M47ToLS3 $sinkP3M47ToLS3
$tcpP3M47ToLS3 set fid_ 3
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP3M47ToLS3 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP3M47ToLS3 attach-agent $tcpP3M47ToLS3
$ftpP3M47ToLS3 set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 3 Maquina 47
set tcpLS3ToP3M47 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpLS3ToP3M47 set class_ 3
$ns attach-agent $P3LS $tcpLS3ToP3M47
set sinkLS3ToP3M47 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P3M47 $sinkLS3ToP3M47
$ns connect $tcpLS3ToP3M47 $sinkLS3ToP3M47
$tcpLS3ToP3M47 set fid_ 3
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpLS3ToP3M47 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpLS3ToP3M47 attach-agent $tcpLS3ToP3M47
$ftpLS3ToP3M47 set type_ FTP

#Create connection TCP Polo 4

#Polo 4 Local Server -- Servidor
set tcpServerToLS4 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToLS4 set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToLS4
set sinkServerToLS4 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P4LS $sinkServerToLS4
$ns connect $tcpServerToLS4 $sinkServerToLS4
$tcpServerToLS4 set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToLS4 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToLS4 attach-agent $tcpServerToLS4
$ftpServerToLS4 set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo local server 4
set tcpLS4ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpLS4ToServer set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $P4LS $tcpLS4ToServer
set sinkLS4ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkLS4ToServer
$ns connect $tcpLS4ToServer $sinkLS4ToServer
$tcpLS4ToServer set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpLS4ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpLS4ToServer attach-agent $tcpLS4ToServer
$ftpLS4ToServer set type_ FTP

set ftpP5M4ToLS5 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP5M4ToLS5 attach-agent $tcpP5M4ToLS5
$ftpP5M4ToLS5 set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 5 Maquina 4
